<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blokiróvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокировка.html>блокиро́вок</a></b>)

<ol><li>blocking, block, blockage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lock</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блокнотик.html>блокно́тик</a> (20063)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блокнот.html>блокно́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bloknót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блоха́</a> (11916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blъxa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰluseh₂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блоха́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bloxá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блохи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>бло́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>бло́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flea
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карман.html>карма́не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блоха.html>блоха́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аркан.html>арка́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá v karmáne <b>bloxá</b> na arkáne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m flat broke.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">I have a <b>flea</b> on a lasso in my pocket.</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>бло<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3d  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> устар. <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 3f:
</p><p><b></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3f  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-блох-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блуд</a> (32131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">блꙋдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bludŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*blǫdъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰlendʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуд.html>блуд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blud</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блуждать.html>блужда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bluždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

<ol><li>to roam, to wander, to rove, to ramble

***блюдо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́до</a> (3126)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bľudo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́до</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bljúdo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́да</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блюд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dish, plate</li>
<li>dish, course
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вятся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рицы</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne nrávjatsja <b>bljúda</b> iz kúricy!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I like chicken!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***блюсти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a> (18478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bľusti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*bjaustei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*bʰewdʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bljustí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюсти.html>соблюсти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to guard, to keep
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> zakóny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to observe the laws; abide by the laws</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́сы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> interésy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to watch over the interests</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> porjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bljustí</b> sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to guard one's chastity; 2) to watch one's waistline; keep in shape</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***бог.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> (254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bogъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">box</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бого́в</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:богиня.html>боги́ня</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>God</li>
<li>god, idol
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>box</b> jevó znájet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God only knows!; goodness knows!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мой</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bóže moj!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">oh God!; good gracious!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>box</b> s nim!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Forget him!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">daj <b>box</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God willing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ей-бо́гу!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jej-bógu!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">really!; really and truly!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́га</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rádi <b>bóga</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for God’s sake!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сохранить.html>сохрани́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́же</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">soxraní bóže!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">save oh Lord!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́гу</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sláva bógu!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">glory to God!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Usually not capitalized in Russian in the sense of idol, or when referring to a single god with a polytheistic pantheon. It is normally capitalized in monotheistic sense, such as in Islamic or Christian discourse (see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>Бог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Box</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), except for some common set expressions<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.</li></ul>
